<div class="chapter" title="Chapter 14. HBase Operational Management" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops_mgt"></a>Chapter 14. HBase 运维管理</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="toc" style="margin:0px">
<p><strong>Table of Contents</strong></p>
<p><strong></strong><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#tools" rel="nofollow">14.1. HBase <span class="title" style="clear:both">工具和实用程序</span></a></span></p>
<p><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#ops.regionmgt" rel="nofollow">14.2. 区域管理</a></span></p>
<p><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#node.management" rel="nofollow">14.3. 节点管理</a></span></p>
<dl style="margin:0.8em 0px; line-height:1.2"><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#hbase_metrics" rel="nofollow">14.4. HBase 度量</a></span></dt><dd> </dd><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#ops.monitoring" rel="nofollow">14.5. HBase 监控</a></span></dt><dd> </dd><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#cluster_replication" rel="nofollow">14.6. 集群复制</a></span></dt><dd> </dd><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#ops.backup" rel="nofollow">14.7. HBase 备份</a></span></dt><dd> </dd><dd><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#ops.backup" rel="nofollow"></a></span><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#ops.backup" rel="nofollow"></a></span><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#ops.backup" rel="nofollow"></a></span></dd><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#ops.capacity" rel="nofollow">14.8. 容量计划</a></span></dt><dd>
<dl style="margin:0.8em 0px; line-height:1.2"><dt> </dt></dl>
</dd></dl>
</div>
This chapter will cover operational tools and practices required of a running HBase cluster. The subject of operations is related to the topics of <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#trouble" rel="nofollow" title="Chapter 12. Troubleshooting and Debugging HBase">Chapter 12, <em>Troubleshooting
 and Debugging HBase</em></a>,<a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#performance" rel="nofollow" title="Chapter 11. Performance Tuning">Chapter 11, <em>Performance Tuning</em></a>, and <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#configuration" rel="nofollow" title="Chapter 2. Configuration">Chapter 2, <em>Configuration</em></a> but
 is a distinct topic in itself.
<div class="section" title="14.1. HBase Tools and Utilities" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px; clear:both">
<a target="_blank" name="tools"></a>14.1. HBase 工具和实用程序</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>这里我们给出HBase工具列表，可用于管理，分析，修复和调试。</p>
<div class="section" title="14.1.1. Driver" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="driver"></a>14.1.1. 驱动</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>There is a <code class="code">Driver</code> class that is executed by the HBase jar can be used to invoke frequently accessed utilities. For example,</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">HADOOP_CLASSPATH=`${HBASE_HOME}/bin/hbase classpath` ${HADOOP_HOME}/bin/hadoop jar ${HBASE_HOME}/hbase-VERSION.jar 
</pre>
<p>... will return...</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">An example program must be given as the first argument.
Valid program names are:
  completebulkload: Complete a bulk data load.
  copytable: Export a table from local cluster to peer cluster
  export: Write table data to HDFS.
  import: Import data written by Export.
  importtsv: Import data in TSV format.
  rowcounter: Count rows in HBase table
  verifyrep: Compare the data from tables in two different clusters. WARNING: It doesn't work for incrementColumnValues'd cells since the timestamp is chan
</pre>
<p>... for allowable program names.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.2. HBase hbck" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbck"></a>14.1.2. HBase <span class="application">hbck</span></h3>
</div>
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="subtitle" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
An <span class="emphasis"><em>fsck</em></span> for your HBase install</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>To run <span class="application">hbck</span> against your HBase cluster run</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ ./bin/hbase hbck</pre>
<p>At the end of the commands output it prints <span class="emphasis"><em>OK</em></span> or <span class="emphasis"><em>INCONSISTENCY</em></span>. If your cluster reports inconsistencies, pass <span class="command"><strong>-details</strong></span> to see more
 detail emitted. If inconsistencies, run <span class="command"><strong>hbck</strong></span> a few times because the inconsistency may be transient (e.g. cluster is starting up or a region is splitting). Passing <span class="command"><strong>-fix</strong></span> may
 correct the inconsistency (This latter is an experimental feature).</p>
<p>For more information, see <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#hbck.in.depth" rel="nofollow" title="Appendix B. hbck In Depth">Appendix B, <em>hbck In Depth</em></a>.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.3. HFile Tool" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hfile_tool2"></a>14.1.3. HFile 工具</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>参考 <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#hfile_tool" rel="nofollow" title="9.7.5.2.2. HFile Tool">Section 9.7.5.2.2, “HFile Tool”</a>.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.4. WAL Tools" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="wal_tools"></a>14.1.4. WAL 工具</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.4.1. HLog tool" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hlog_tool"></a>14.1.4.1. <code class="classname">HLog</code> tool</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The main method on <code class="classname">HLog</code> offers manual split and dump facilities. Pass it WALs or the product of a split, the content of the <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">recovered.edits</code>. directory.</p>
<p>You can get a textual dump of a WAL file content by doing the following:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)"> <code class="code">$ ./bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.regionserver.wal.HLog --dump hdfs://example.org:8020/hbase/.logs/example.org,60020,1283516293161/10.10.21.10%3A60020.1283973724012</code> </pre>
<p>The return code will be non-zero if issues with the file so you can test wholesomeness of file by redirecting <code class="varname">STDOUT</code> to <code class="code">/dev/null</code> and testing the program return.</p>
<p>Similarly you can force a split of a log file directory by doing:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)"> $ ./<code class="code">bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.regionserver.wal.HLog --split hdfs://example.org:8020/hbase/.logs/example.org,60020,1283516293161/</code></pre>
<div class="section" title="14.1.4.1.1. HLogPrettyPrinter" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h5 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -31.203125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hlog_tool.prettyprint"></a>14.1.4.1.1. <code class="classname">HLogPrettyPrinter</code></h5>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><code class="classname">HLogPrettyPrinter</code> is a tool with configurable options to print the contents of an HLog.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.5. Compression Tool" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="compression.tool"></a>14.1.5. Compression Tool</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>参考 <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#compression.test" rel="nofollow" title="C.1. CompressionTest Tool">Section C.1, “CompressionTest Tool”</a>.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.6. CopyTable" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="copytable"></a>14.1.6. CopyTable</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>CopyTable is a utility that can copy part or of all of a table, either to the same cluster or another cluster. The usage is as follows:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.mapreduce.CopyTable [--starttime=X] [--endtime=Y] [--new.name=NEW] [--peer.adr=ADR] tablename
</pre>
<p></p>
<p>Options:</p>
<div class="itemizedlist" style="margin:0px">
<ul class="itemizedlist" type="disc" style="margin:0px 0px 0px 78.015625px; line-height:1.2">
<li class="listitem"><code class="varname">starttime</code> Beginning of the time range. Without endtime means starttime to forever.</li><li class="listitem"><code class="varname">endtime</code> End of the time range. Without endtime means starttime to forever.</li><li class="listitem"><code class="varname">versions</code> Number of cell versions to copy.</li><li class="listitem"><code class="varname">new.name</code> New table's name.</li><li class="listitem"><code class="varname">peer.adr</code> Address of the peer cluster given in the format hbase.zookeeper.quorum:hbase.zookeeper.client.port:zookeeper.znode.parent</li><li class="listitem"><code class="varname">families</code> Comma-separated list of ColumnFamilies to copy.</li><li class="listitem"><code class="varname">all.cells</code> Also copy delete markers and uncollected deleted cells (advanced option).</li></ul>
</div>
<p>Args:</p>
<div class="itemizedlist" style="margin:0px">
<ul class="itemizedlist" type="disc" style="margin:0px 0px 0px 78.015625px; line-height:1.2">
<li class="listitem">tablename Name of table to copy.</li></ul>
</div>
<p></p>
<p>Example of copying 'TestTable' to a cluster that uses replication for a 1 hour window:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.mapreduce.CopyTable
--starttime=1265875194289 --endtime=1265878794289
--peer.adr=server1,server2,server3:2181:/hbase TestTable</pre>
<p></p>
<div class="note" title="Scanner Caching" style="margin:0px 0.5in">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -43.921875px">
Scanner Caching</h3>
<p>Caching for the input Scan is configured via <code class="code">hbase.client.scanner.caching</code> in the job configuration.</p>
</div>
<p>参考 Jonathan Hsieh's <a target="_blank" class="link" href="http://www.cloudera.com/blog/2012/06/online-hbase-backups-with-copytable-2/" rel="nofollow">Online HBase Backups with CopyTable</a> blog post for more on <span class="command"><strong>CopyTable</strong></span>.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.7. Export" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="export"></a>14.1.7. 导出</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>导出实用工具可以将表的内容输出成HDFS的序列化文件，如下调用：</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.mapreduce.Export &lt;tablename&gt; &lt;outputdir&gt; [&lt;versions&gt; [&lt;starttime&gt; [&lt;endtime&gt;]]]
</pre>
<p></p>
<p>Note: caching for the input Scan is configured via <code class="code">hbase.client.scanner.caching</code> in the job configuration.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.8. Import" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="import"></a>14.1.8. 导入</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>导入实用工具可以加载导出的数据回到HBase，如下调用：</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.mapreduce.Import &lt;tablename&gt; &lt;inputdir&gt;
</pre>
<p></p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.9. ImportTsv" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="importtsv"></a>14.1.9. ImportTsv</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>ImportTsv is a utility that will load data in TSV format into HBase. It has two distinct usages: loading data from TSV format in HDFS into HBase via Puts, and preparing StoreFiles to be loaded via the <code class="code">completebulkload</code>.</p>
<p>To load data via Puts (i.e., non-bulk loading):</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.mapreduce.ImportTsv -Dimporttsv.columns=a,b,c &lt;tablename&gt; &lt;hdfs-inputdir&gt;
</pre>
<p></p>
<p>To generate StoreFiles for bulk-loading:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.mapreduce.ImportTsv -Dimporttsv.columns=a,b,c -Dimporttsv.bulk.output=hdfs://storefile-outputdir &lt;tablename&gt; &lt;hdfs-data-inputdir&gt;
</pre>
<p></p>
<p>These generated StoreFiles can be loaded into HBase via <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#completebulkload" rel="nofollow" title="14.1.10. CompleteBulkLoad">Section 14.1.10, “CompleteBulkLoad”</a>.</p>
<div class="section" title="14.1.9.1. ImportTsv Options" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="importtsv.options"></a>14.1.9.1. ImportTsv 选项</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
Running ImportTsv with no arguments prints brief usage information:
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">Usage: importtsv -Dimporttsv.columns=a,b,c &lt;tablename&gt; &lt;inputdir&gt;

Imports the given input directory of TSV data into the specified table.

The column names of the TSV data must be specified using the -Dimporttsv.columns
option. This option takes the form of comma-separated column names, where each
column name is either a simple column family, or a columnfamily:qualifier. The special
column name HBASE_ROW_KEY is used to designate that this column should be used
as the row key for each imported record. You must specify exactly one column
to be the row key, and you must specify a column name for every column that exists in the
input data.

By default importtsv will load data directly into HBase. To instead generate
HFiles of data to prepare for a bulk data load, pass the option:
  -Dimporttsv.bulk.output=/path/for/output
  Note: if you do not use this option, then the target table must already exist in HBase

Other options that may be specified with -D include:
  -Dimporttsv.skip.bad.lines=false - fail if encountering an invalid line
  '-Dimporttsv.separator=|' - eg separate on pipes instead of tabs
  -Dimporttsv.timestamp=currentTimeAsLong - use the specified timestamp for the import
  -Dimporttsv.mapper.class=my.Mapper - A user-defined Mapper to use instead of org.apache.hadoop.hbase.mapreduce.TsvImporterMapper
</pre>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.9.2. ImportTsv Example" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="importtsv.example"></a>14.1.9.2. ImportTsv 示例</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>For example, assume that we are loading data into a table called 'datatsv' with a ColumnFamily called 'd' with two columns "c1" and "c2".</p>
<p>Assume that an input file exists as follows:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">row1	c1	c2
row2	c1	c2
row3	c1	c2
row4	c1	c2
row5	c1	c2
row6	c1	c2
row7	c1	c2
row8	c1	c2
row9	c1	c2
row10	c1	c2
</pre>
<p></p>
<p>For ImportTsv to use this imput file, the command line needs to look like this:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)"> HADOOP_CLASSPATH=`${HBASE_HOME}/bin/hbase classpath` ${HADOOP_HOME}/bin/hadoop jar ${HBASE_HOME}/hbase-VERSION.jar importtsv -Dimporttsv.columns=HBASE_ROW_KEY,d:c1,d:c2 -Dimporttsv.bulk.output=hdfs://storefileoutput  datatsv hdfs://inputfile
 </pre>
<p>... and in this example the first column is the rowkey, which is why the HBASE_ROW_KEY is used. The second and third columns in the file will be imported as "d:c1" and "d:c2", respectively.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.9.3. ImportTsv Warning" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="importtsv.warning"></a>14.1.9.3. ImportTsv Warning</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>If you have preparing a lot of data for bulk loading, make sure the target HBase table is pre-split appropriately.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.9.4. See Also" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="importtsv.also"></a>14.1.9.4. 参考</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
For more information about bulk-loading HFiles into HBase, see <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#arch.bulk.load" rel="nofollow" title="9.8. Bulk Loading">Section 9.8, “Bulk Loading”</a></div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.10. CompleteBulkLoad" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="completebulkload"></a>14.1.10. CompleteBulkLoad</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><code class="code">completebulkload</code> 实用工具可以将产生的存储文件移动到HBase表。该工具经常和<a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#importtsv" rel="nofollow" title="14.1.9. ImportTsv">Section 14.1.9, “ImportTsv”</a> 的输出联合使用。</p>
<p>两种方法调用该工具，带显式类名或通过驱动：</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.mapreduce.LoadIncrementalHFiles &lt;hdfs://storefileoutput&gt; &lt;tablename&gt;
</pre>
<p>.. 通过驱动..</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">HADOOP_CLASSPATH=`${HBASE_HOME}/bin/hbase classpath` ${HADOOP_HOME}/bin/hadoop jar ${HBASE_HOME}/hbase-VERSION.jar completebulkload &lt;hdfs://storefileoutput&gt; &lt;tablename&gt;
</pre>
<p></p>
<p>批量导入 HFiles 到 HBase的更多信息 ，参考 <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#arch.bulk.load" rel="nofollow" title="9.8. Bulk Loading">Section 9.8, “Bulk Loading”</a>.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.11. WALPlayer" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="walplayer"></a>14.1.11. WALPlayer</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>WALPlayer 实用工具可以重放 WAL 文件到 HBase.</p>
<p>The WAL can be replayed for a set of tables or all tables, and a timerange can be provided (in milliseconds). The WAL is filtered to this set of tables. The output can optionally be mapped to another set of tables.</p>
<p>WALPlayer can also generate HFiles for later bulk importing, in that case only a single table and no mapping can be specified.</p>
<p>Invoke via:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.mapreduce.WALPlayer [options] &lt;wal inputdir&gt; &lt;tables&gt; [&lt;tableMappings&gt;]&gt;
</pre>
<p></p>
<p>For example:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.mapreduce.WALPlayer /backuplogdir oldTable1,oldTable2 newTable1,newTable2
</pre>
<p></p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.1.12. RowCounter" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="rowcounter"></a>14.1.12. RowCounter</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>RowCounter 实用工具可以统计表的行数。这是一个好工具，如果担心元数据可能存在不一致，可以用于确认HBase可以读取表的所有分块。</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ bin/hbase org.apache.hadoop.hbase.mapreduce.RowCounter &lt;tablename&gt; [&lt;column1&gt; &lt;column2&gt;...]
</pre>
<p></p>
<p>Note: caching for the input Scan is configured via <code class="code">hbase.client.scanner.caching</code> in the job configuration.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.2. Region Management" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px; clear:both">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.regionmgt"></a>14.2. 区域管理</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.2.1. Major Compaction" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.regionmgt.majorcompact"></a>14.2.1. 主紧缩</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>主紧缩可以通过HBase shell 或 <a target="_blank" class="link" href="http://hbase.apache.org/apidocs/org/apache/hadoop/hbase/client/HBaseAdmin.html#majorCompact%28java.lang.String%29" rel="nofollow">HBaseAdmin.majorCompact</a> 进行。</p>
<p>注意：主紧缩<strong><em>不</em></strong>进行区域合并。更多关于紧缩的信息，参考 <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#compaction" rel="nofollow" title="9.7.5.5. Compaction">Section 9.7.5.5, “Compaction”</a></p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.2.2. Merge" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.regionmgt.merge"></a>14.2.2. 合并</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Merge is a utility that can merge adjoining regions in the same table (see org.apache.hadoop.hbase.util.Merge).</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ bin/hbase org.apache.hbase.util.Merge &lt;tablename&gt; &lt;region1&gt; &lt;region2&gt;
</pre>
<p>If you feel you have too many regions and want to consolidate them, Merge is the utility you need. Merge must run be done when the cluster is down. 参考 the <a target="_blank" class="link" href="http://ofps.oreilly.com/titles/9781449396107/performance.html" rel="nofollow">O'Reilly
 HBase Book</a> for an example of usage.</p>
<p>Additionally, there is a Ruby script attached to <a target="_blank" class="link" href="https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/HBASE-1621" rel="nofollow">HBASE-1621</a> for region merging.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.3. Node Management" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px; clear:both">
<a target="_blank" name="node.management"></a>14.3. 节点管理</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.3.1. Node Decommission" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="decommission"></a>14.3.1. 节点下线</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>你可以在HBase的特定的节点上运行下面的脚本来停止RegionServer:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ ./bin/hbase-daemon.sh stop regionserver</pre>
<p>RegionServer会首先关闭所有的region然后把它自己关闭，在停止的过程中，RegionServer的会向Zookeeper报告说他已经过期了。master会发现RegionServer已经死了，会把它当作崩溃的server来处理。他会将region分配到其他的节点上去。</p>
<div class="note" title="在下线节点之前要停止Load Balancer" style="margin:0px 0.5in">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -43.921875px">
在下线节点之前要停止Load Balancer</h3>
<p>如果在运行load balancer的时候，一个节点要关闭， 则Load Balancer和Master的recovery可能会争夺这个要下线的Regionserver。为了避免这个问题，先将load balancer停止，参见下面的 <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#lb" rel="nofollow" title="Load Balancer">Load Balancer</a>.</p>
</div>
<p></p>
<p>RegionServer下线有一个缺点就是其中的Region会有好一会离线。Regions是被按顺序关闭的。如果一个server上有很多region,从第一个region会被下线，到最后一个region被关闭，并且Master确认他已经死了，该region才可以上线，整个过程要花很长时间。在HBase 0.90.2中，我们加入了一个功能，可以让节点逐渐的摆脱他的负载，最后关闭。HBase 0.90.2加入了 <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">graceful_stop.sh</code>脚本，可以这样用，</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ ./bin/graceful_stop.sh 
Usage: graceful_stop.sh [--config &amp;conf-dir&gt;] [--restart] [--reload] [--thrift] [--rest] &amp;hostname&gt;
 thrift      If we should stop/start thrift before/after the hbase stop/start
 rest        If we should stop/start rest before/after the hbase stop/start
 restart     If we should restart after graceful stop
 reload      Move offloaded regions back on to the stopped server
 debug       Move offloaded regions back on to the stopped server
 hostname    Hostname of server we are to stop</pre>
<p></p>
<p>要下线一台RegionServer可以这样做</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ ./bin/graceful_stop.sh HOSTNAME</pre>
<p>这里的<code class="varname">HOSTNAME</code>是RegionServer的host you would decommission.</p>
<div class="note" title="On HOSTNAME" style="margin:0px 0.5in">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -43.921875px">
On <code class="varname">HOSTNAME</code></h3>
<p>传递到<code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">graceful_stop.sh</code>的<code class="varname">HOSTNAME</code>必须和hbase使用的hostname一致，hbase用它来区分RegionServers。可以用master的UI来检查RegionServers的id。通常是hostname,也可能是FQDN。不管HBase使用的哪一个，你可以将它传到 <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">graceful_stop.sh</code>脚本中去，目前他还不支持使用IP地址来推断hostname。所以使用IP就会发现server不在运行，也没有办法下线了。</p>
</div>
<p><code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">graceful_stop.sh</code> 脚本会一个一个将region从RegionServer中移除出去，以减少改RegionServer的负载。他会先移除一个region,然后再将这个region安置到一个新的地方，再移除下一个，直到全部移除。最后<code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">graceful_stop.sh</code>脚本会让RegionServer <span class="command"><strong>stop</strong></span>.,Master会注意到RegionServer已经下线了，这个时候所有的region已经重新部署好。RegionServer就可以干干净净的结束，没有WAL日志需要分割。</p>
<div class="note" title="Load Balancer" style="margin:0px 0.5in">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -43.921875px">
<a target="_blank" name="lb"></a>Load Balancer</h3>
<p>当执行<span class="command"><strong>graceful_stop</strong></span>脚本的时候，要将Region Load Balancer关掉(否则balancer和下线脚本会在region部署的问题上存在冲突):</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">hbase(main):001:0&gt; balance_switch false
true
0 row(s) in 0.3590 seconds</pre>
<p>上面是将balancer关掉，要想开启：</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">hbase(main):001:0&gt; balance_switch true
false
0 row(s) in 0.3590 seconds</pre>
<p></p>
</div>
<p></p>
<div class="note" title="Load Balancer" style="margin:0px 0.5in">
<p></p>
</div>
<p></p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.3.2. Rolling Restart" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="rolling"></a>14.3.2. 依次重启</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>你还可以让这个脚本重启一个RegionServer,不改变上面的Region的位置。要想保留数据的位置，你可以依次重启(Rolling Restart),就像这样:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ for i in `cat conf/regionservers|sort`; do ./bin/graceful_stop.sh --restart --reload --debug $i; done &amp;&gt; /tmp/log.txt &amp;
            </pre>
<p>Tail <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">/tmp/log.txt</code>来看脚本的运行过程.上面的脚本只对RegionServer进行操作。要确认load balancer已经关掉。还需要在之前更新master。下面是一段依次重启的伪脚本,你可以借鉴它：</p>
<div class="orderedlist" style="margin:0px">
<ol class="orderedlist" type="1" style="margin:0px 0px 0px 78.015625px; line-height:1.2">
<li class="listitem">
<p>确认你的版本，保证配置已经rsync到整个集群中。如果版本是0.90.2，需要打上HBASE-3744 和 HBASE-3756两个补丁。</p>
</li><li class="listitem">
<p>运行hbck确保你的集群是一致的</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ ./bin/hbase hbck</pre>
<p>当发现不一致的时候，可以修复他。</p>
</li><li class="listitem">
<p>重启Master:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ ./bin/hbase-daemon.sh stop master; ./bin/hbase-daemon.sh start master</pre>
<p></p>
</li><li class="listitem">
<p>关闭region balancer:</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ echo "balance_switch false" | ./bin/hbase</pre>
<p></p>
</li><li class="listitem">
<p>在每个RegionServer上运行<code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">graceful_stop.sh</code>：</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">$ for i in `cat conf/regionservers|sort`; do ./bin/graceful_stop.sh --restart --reload --debug $i; done &amp;&gt; /tmp/log.txt &amp;
            </pre>
<p>如果你在RegionServer还开起来thrift和rest server。还需要加上--thrift or --rest 选项 (参见 <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">graceful_stop.sh</code> 脚本的用法).</p>
</li><li class="listitem">
<p>再次重启Master.这会把已经死亡的server列表清空，重新开启balancer.</p>
</li><li class="listitem">
<p>运行 hbck 保证集群是一直的</p>
</li></ol>
</div>
<div class="orderedlist" style="margin:0px"></div>
<p></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4. HBase Metrics" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px; clear:both">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase_metrics"></a>14.4. HBase 度量</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.1. Metric Setup" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="metric_setup"></a>14.4.1. 度量<span class="title" style="clear:both">安装</span></h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>参见 <a target="_blank" class="link" href="http://hbase.apache.org/metrics.html" rel="nofollow">Metrics</a> 可以获得一个enable Metrics emission的指导。</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2. RegionServer Metrics" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="rs_metrics"></a>14.4.2. 区域服务器度量</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.1. hbase.regionserver.blockCacheCount" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.blockCacheCount"></a>14.4.2.1. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.blockCacheCount</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>内存中的Block cache item数量。这个是存储文件(HFiles)的缓存中的数量。</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.2. hbase.regionserver.blockCacheEvictedCount" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.blockCacheEvictedCount"></a>14.4.2.2. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.blockCacheEvictedCount</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Number of blocks that had to be evicted from the block cache due to heap size constraints.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.3. hbase.regionserver.blockCacheFree" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.blockCacheFree"></a>14.4.2.3. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.blockCacheFree</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>内存中的Block cache memory 剩余 (单位 bytes).</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.4. hbase.regionserver.blockCacheHitCachingRatio" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.blockCacheHitCachingRatio"></a>14.4.2.4. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.blockCacheHitCachingRatio</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Block cache hit caching ratio (0 to 100). The cache-hit ratio for reads configured to look in the cache (i.e., cacheBlocks=true).</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.5. hbase.regionserver.blockCacheHitCount" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.blockCacheHitCount"></a>14.4.2.5. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.blockCacheHitCount</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Number of blocks of StoreFiles (HFiles) read from the cache.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.6. hbase.regionserver.blockCacheHitRatio" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.blockCacheHitRatio"></a>14.4.2.6. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.blockCacheHitRatio</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Block cache 命中率(0 到 100). Includes all read requests, although those with cacheBlocks=false will always read from disk and be counted as a "cache miss"</p>
<p> </p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.7. hbase.regionserver.blockCacheMissCount" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.blockCacheMissCount"></a>14.4.2.7. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.blockCacheMissCount</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>StoreFiles (HFiles)请求的未在缓存中的分块数量。</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.8. hbase.regionserver.blockCacheSize" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.blockCacheSize"></a>14.4.2.8. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.blockCacheSize</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>内存中的Block cache 大小 (单位 bytes). i.e., memory in use by the BlockCache</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.9. hbase.regionserver.compactionQueueSize" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.compactionQueueSize"></a>14.4.2.9. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.compactionQueueSize</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>compaction队列的大小. 这个值是需要进行compaction的region数目</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.10. hbase.regionserver.flushQueueSize" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.flushQueueSize"></a>14.4.2.10. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.flushQueueSize</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Number of enqueued regions in the MemStore awaiting flush.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.11. hbase.regionserver.fsReadLatency_avg_time" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.fsReadLatency_avg_time"></a>14.4.2.11. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.fsReadLatency_avg_time</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>文件系统延迟 (ms). 这个值是平均读HDFS的延迟时间</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.12. hbase.regionserver.fsReadLatency_num_ops" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.fsReadLatency_num_ops"></a>14.4.2.12. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.fsReadLatency_num_ops</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>文件系统读操作。</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.13. hbase.regionserver.fsSyncLatency_avg_time" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.fsSyncLatency_avg_time"></a>14.4.2.13. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.fsSyncLatency_avg_time</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>文件系统同步延迟(ms). Latency to sync the write-ahead log records to the filesystem.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.14. hbase.regionserver.fsSyncLatency_num_ops" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.fsSyncLatency_num_ops"></a>14.4.2.14. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.fsSyncLatency_num_ops</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Number of operations to sync the write-ahead log records to the filesystem.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.15. hbase.regionserver.fsWriteLatency_avg_time" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.fsWriteLatency_avg_time"></a>14.4.2.15. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.fsWriteLatency_avg_time</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>文件系统写延迟(ms). Total latency for all writers, including StoreFiles and write-head log.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.16. hbase.regionserver.fsWriteLatency_num_ops" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.fsWriteLatency_num_ops"></a>14.4.2.16. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.fsWriteLatency_num_ops</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Number of filesystem write operations, including StoreFiles and write-ahead log.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.17. hbase.regionserver.memstoreSizeMB" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.memstoreSizeMB"></a>14.4.2.17. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.memstoreSizeMB</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>所有的RegionServer的memstore大小 (MB)</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.18. hbase.regionserver.regions" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.regions"></a>14.4.2.18. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.regions</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>RegionServer服务的regions数量</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.19. hbase.regionserver.requests" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.requests"></a>14.4.2.19. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.requests</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>读写请求的全部数量。请求是指RegionServer的RPC数量，因此一次Get一个请求，但一个缓存设为1000的Scan也会在每次调用'next'时导致一个请求。一个批量load是一个Hfile一个请求。</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.20. hbase.regionserver.storeFileIndexSizeMB" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.storeFileIndexSizeMB"></a>14.4.2.20. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.storeFileIndexSizeMB</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>当前RegionServer的storefile索引的总大小(MB)</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.21. hbase.regionserver.stores" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.stores"></a>14.4.2.21. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.stores</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>RegionServer打开的stores数量。一个stores对应一个列族。例如，一个包含列族的表有3个region在这个RegionServer上，对应一个 列族就会有3个store.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.4.2.22. hbase.regionserver.storeFiles" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="hbase.regionserver.storeFiles"></a>14.4.2.22. <code class="varname">hbase.regionserver.storeFiles</code></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>RegionServer打开的存储文件(HFile)数量。这个值一定大于等于store的数量。</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.5. HBase Monitoring" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px; clear:both">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.monitoring"></a>14.5. HBase 监控</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.5.1. Overview" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.monitoring.overview"></a>14.5.1. 概述</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>下面的度量方法对每个区域服务器的宏观监控被证明是是最重要的，特别是在像 <a target="_blank" class="link" href="http://opentsdb.net/" rel="nofollow">OpenTSDB</a>这样的系统中。如果你的集群具有性能问题，你可能得参考本组信息。</p>
<p>HBase:</p>
<div class="itemizedlist" style="margin:0px">
<ul class="itemizedlist" type="disc" style="margin:0px 0px 0px 78.015625px; line-height:1.2">
<li class="listitem">Requests</li><li class="listitem">Compactions queue</li></ul>
</div>
<p></p>
<p>OS:</p>
<div class="itemizedlist" style="margin:0px">
<ul class="itemizedlist" type="disc" style="margin:0px 0px 0px 78.015625px; line-height:1.2">
<li class="listitem">IO Wait</li><li class="listitem">User CPU</li></ul>
</div>
<p></p>
<p>Java:</p>
<div class="itemizedlist" style="margin:0px">
<ul class="itemizedlist" type="disc" style="margin:0px 0px 0px 78.015625px; line-height:1.2">
<li class="listitem">GC</li></ul>
</div>
<p></p>
<p></p>
<p>HBase度量的更多信息，参考 <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#hbase_metrics" rel="nofollow" title="14.4. HBase Metrics">Section 14.4, “HBase Metrics”</a>.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.5.2. Slow Query Log" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.slow.query"></a>14.5.2. 查询太慢的日志</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>HBase查询太慢的日志由可分析的 JSON结构描述。客户端操作 (Gets, Puts, Deletes, 等)的属性， 要么运行太久，或产生输出太多。“运行太久”和“输出太多”的门限可配置，如后面所述。输出产生在主区域服务器日志中，以便和其他日志事件一起发现更多细节。它也前置区分标签<code class="constant">(responseTooSlow)</code>, <code class="constant">(responseTooLarge)</code>, <code class="constant">(operationTooSlow)</code>和<code class="constant">(operationTooLarge)</code>，以便当用户只希望看到慢查询时，用grep过滤。</p>
<div class="section" title="14.5.2.1. Configuration" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="d1952e9354"></a>14.5.2.1. 配置</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>有两个配置节可用于调整查询太慢日志的门限。</p>
<div class="itemizedlist" style="margin:0px">
<ul class="itemizedlist" type="disc" style="margin:0px 0px 0px 78.015625px; line-height:1.2">
<li class="listitem"><code class="varname">hbase.ipc.warn.response.time</code> 不被记录太慢日志的查询执行的最大毫秒数(millisecond) 。缺省10000, 即 10 秒。可设 -1 禁止通过时间长短记入日志。</li><li class="listitem"><code class="varname">hbase.ipc.warn.response.size</code> 不被记录日志的查询可返回的最大字节数。缺省 100 MB，可设为 -1 禁止通过大小记入日志。</li></ul>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.5.2.2. Metrics" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="d1952e9368"></a>14.5.2.2. 度量</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>查询太慢日志暴露给了JMX 度量。</p>
<div class="itemizedlist" style="margin:0px">
<ul class="itemizedlist" type="disc" style="margin:0px 0px 0px 78.015625px; line-height:1.2">
<li class="listitem"><code class="varname">hadoop.regionserver_rpc_slowResponse</code> 是一个全局度量，反射所有超时记入日志的响应。</li><li class="listitem"><code class="varname">hadoop.regionserver_rpc_methodName.aboveOneSec</code> 一个度量，反射所有超过一秒时间的响应。</li></ul>
</div>
<p></p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.5.2.3. Output" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="d1952e9383"></a>14.5.2.3. 输出</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>输出以操作做标签，如 <code class="constant">(operationTooSlow)</code> 。如果调用是客户端操作，如 Put, Get, 或 Delete，会暴露详细指纹信息。否则，标签为 <code class="constant">(responseTooSlow)</code> ，也同样提供可分析的JSON 输出，但具有较少细节信息，完全依赖于RPC自身的超时和超量设置。 <code class="constant">TooLarge</code> 代替 <code class="constant">TooSlow</code> 如果响应大小引起日志记录。在大小和时长都引起日志记录时，也是 <code class="constant">TooLarge</code> 后置。</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.5.2.4. Example" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="d1952e9403"></a>14.5.2.4. 示例</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p></p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">2011-09-08 10:01:25,824 WARN org.apache.hadoop.ipc.HBaseServer: (operationTooSlow): {"tables":{"riley2":{"puts":[{"totalColumns":11,"families":{"actions":[{"timestamp":1315501284459,"qualifier":"0","vlen":9667580},{"timestamp":1315501284459,"qualifier":"1","vlen":10122412},{"timestamp":1315501284459,"qualifier":"2","vlen":11104617},{"timestamp":1315501284459,"qualifier":"3","vlen":13430635}]},"row":"cfcd208495d565ef66e7dff9f98764da:0"}],"families":["actions"]}},"processingtimems":956,"client":"10.47.34.63:33623","starttimems":1315501284456,"queuetimems":0,"totalPuts":1,"class":"HRegionServer","responsesize":0,"method":"multiPut"}</pre>
<p></p>
<p>注意，在"tables"结构里的所有东西，是MultiPut的指纹打印的输出。其余的信息是RPC相关的，如处理时间和客户端IP/port。 客户端的其他操作的模式和通用结构与此相同，但根据单个操作的类型会有一定的不同。如果调用不是客户端操作，则指纹细节信息将完全没有。</p>
<p>对本示例而言，指出了缓慢的原因可能是简单的超大 ( 100MB) multiput，通过 "vlen" 即 value length告知，multiPut中的每个put的域有该信息。</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.6. Cluster Replication" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px; clear:both">
<a target="_blank" name="cluster_replication"></a>14.6. 集群复制</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>参见 <a target="_blank" class="link" href="http://hbase.apache.org/replication.html" rel="nofollow">集群复制</a>.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.7. HBase Backup" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px; clear:both">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.backup"></a>14.7. HBase 备份</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>有两种通常策略进行 HBase 备份：停止整个集群再备份，和在正在使用的集群上备份。 每一种途径都有优缺点。</p>
<p>更多信息，参考Sematext的Blog <a target="_blank" class="link" href="http://blog.sematext.com/2011/03/11/hbase-backup-options/" rel="nofollow">HBase Backup Options</a>.</p>
<div class="section" title="14.7.1. Full Shutdown Backup" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.backup.fullshutdown"></a>14.7.1. 全停止备份</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>一些环境可以容忍暂时停止 HBase 集群，如用于后台容量分析，并不提供前台页面。 好处是 NameNode/Master 和 RegionServers是停止的， 不会有任何机会丢失正在处理改变的保存文件或元数据。明显的坏处是集群被 关闭。步骤包括：</p>
<div class="section" title="14.7.1.1. Stop HBase" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.backup.fullshutdown.stop"></a>14.7.1.1. 停止 HBase</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p></p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.7.1.2. Distcp" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.backup.fullshutdown.distcp"></a>14.7.1.2. Distcp</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Distcp 既用于将HDFS里面的HBase 目录下的内容拷贝到当前集群的另一个目录，也可以拷贝到另一个集群。</p>
<p>注意： Distcp 工作的情形是集群关闭，没有正在改变的文件。Distcp 不推荐用于正工作着的集群。</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.7.1.3. Restore (if needed)" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.backup.fullshutdown.restore"></a>14.7.1.3. 恢复 (如有必要)</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>通过distcp，从 HDFS备份的数据被拷贝到 '真实' 的hbase 目录。 复制动作产生新的 HDFS 元数据， 所以并不需要从备份的NameNode 元数据恢复, 因为是通过distcp从一个特定的 HDFS 目录 (如, HBase 部分)复制， 不是整个HDFS 文件系统。</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.7.2. Live Cluster Backup - Replication" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.backup.live.replication"></a>14.7.2. 工作集群备份 - Replication</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>这种方法假设有另一个集群。参考HBase的 <a target="_blank" class="link" href="http://hbase.apache.org/replication.html" rel="nofollow">replication</a> 。</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.7.3. Live Cluster Backup - CopyTable" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.backup.live.copytable"></a>14.7.3. 工作集群备份 - CopyTable</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#copytable" rel="nofollow" title="14.1.6. CopyTable"> 14.1.6节, “CopyTable”</a> 工具，即可用于将一个表复制到同集群的另一个表，也可将表复制到另一个集群的另一个表。</p>
<p>由于集群在工作，有丢失正在改变的数据的风险。</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.7.4. Live Cluster Backup - Export" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.backup.live.export"></a>14.7.4. 工作集群备份 - Export</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#export" rel="nofollow" title="14.1.7. Export"> 14.1.7节, “Export”</a> 是一种将 HDFS 内容导出到同一集群的方法。 恢复数据， <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#import" rel="nofollow" title="14.1.8. Import">14.1.8节,
 “Import”</a> 工具可以使用。</p>
<p>由于集群在工作，有丢失正在改变的数据的风险。</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.8. Capacity Planning" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px; clear:both">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.capacity"></a>14.8. 容量计划</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.8.1. Storage" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.capacity.storage"></a>14.8.1.存储</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>一个常见问题是HBase管理员需要估算一个HBase集群要用多大存储量。可以通过几个方面去考虑，最重要的是集群要加载什么数据。 开始于对HBase内部处理数据(KeyValue)的可靠了解。</p>
<div class="section" title="14.8.1.1. KeyValue" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.capacity.storage.kv"></a>14.8.1.1. KeyValue</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>HBase storage will be dominated by KeyValues. 参考 <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#keyvalue" rel="nofollow" title="9.7.5.4. KeyValue">Section 9.7.5.4, “KeyValue”</a> and <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#keysize" rel="nofollow" title="6.3.2. Try to minimize row and column sizes">Section 6.3.2,
 “Try to minimize row and column sizes”</a> for how HBase stores data internally.</p>
<p>It is critical to understand that there is a KeyValue instance for every attribute stored in a row, and the rowkey-length, ColumnFamily name-length and attribute lengths will drive the size of the database more than any other factor.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.8.1.2. StoreFiles and Blocks" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.capacity.storage.sf"></a>14.8.1.2. StoreFiles and Blocks</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>KeyValue instances are aggregated into blocks, and the blocksize is configurable on a per-ColumnFamily basis. Blocks are aggregated into StoreFile's. 参考 <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#regions.arch" rel="nofollow" title="9.7. Regions">Section 9.7,
 “Regions”</a>.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.8.1.3. HDFS Block Replication" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.capacity.storage.hdfs"></a>14.8.1.3. HDFS Block Replication</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Because HBase runs on top of HDFS, factor in HDFS block replication into storage calculations.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="14.8.2. Regions" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="ops.capacity.regions"></a>14.8.2. 区域</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Another common question for HBase administrators is determining the right number of regions per RegionServer. This affects both storage and hardware planning. 参考 <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#perf.number.of.regions" rel="nofollow" title="11.4.1. Number of Regions">Section 11.4.1,
 “Number of Regions”</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="chapter" title="Chapter 15. Building and Developing HBase" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px">
<a target="_blank" name="developer"></a>Chapter 15. 创建和部署HBase</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>

Adding an HBase release to Apache's Maven Repository</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#build.gotchas" rel="nofollow">15.3.5. </dd><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#hbase.site" rel="nofollow">15.4. Updating hbase.apache.org</a></span></dt><dd>
<dl style="margin:0.8em 0px; line-height:1.2"><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#hbase.site.contributing" rel="nofollow">15.4.1. Contributing to hbase.apache.org</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#hbase.site.publishing" rel="nofollow">15.4.2. Publishing hbase.apache.org</a></span></dt></dl>
</dd><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#hbase.tests" rel="nofollow">15.6. Tests</a></span></dt><dd>
<dl style="margin:0.8em 0px; line-height:1.2"><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#hbase.moduletests" rel="nofollow">15.6.1. HBase Modules</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#hbase.unittests" rel="nofollow">15.6.2. Unit Tests</a></span></dt></dl>
</dd><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#maven.build.commands" rel="nofollow">15.7. Maven Build Commands</a></span></dt><dd>
<dl style="margin:0.8em 0px; line-height:1.2"><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#maven.build.commands.compile" rel="nofollow">15.7.1. Compile</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#maven.build.commands.unitall" rel="nofollow">15.7.2. Running all or individual Unit Tests</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#maven.build.hadoop" rel="nofollow">15.7.3. Building against various hadoop versions.</a></span></dt></dl>
</dd><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#getting.involved" rel="nofollow">15.8. Getting Involved</a></span></dt><dd>
<dl style="margin:0.8em 0px; line-height:1.2"><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#mailing.list" rel="nofollow">15.8.1. Mailing Lists</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#jira" rel="nofollow">15.8.2. Jira</a></span></dt></dl>
</dd><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#developing" rel="nofollow">15.9. Developing</a></span></dt><dd>
<dl style="margin:0.8em 0px; line-height:1.2"><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#codelines" rel="nofollow">15.9.1. Codelines</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#unit.tests" rel="nofollow">15.9.2. Unit Tests</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#code.standards" rel="nofollow">15.9.3. Code Standards</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#run.insitu" rel="nofollow">15.9.4. Running In-Situ</a></span></dt></dl>
</dd><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#submitting.patches" rel="nofollow">15.10. Submitting Patches</a></span></dt><dd>
<dl style="margin:0.8em 0px; line-height:1.2"><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#submitting.patches.create" rel="nofollow">15.10.1. Create Patch</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#submitting.patches.naming" rel="nofollow">15.10.2. Unit Tests</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#submitting.patches.jira" rel="nofollow">15.10.4. Attach Patch to Jira</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#common.patch.feedback" rel="nofollow">15.10.5. Common Patch Feedback</a></span></dt><dt><span class="section"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#reviewboard" rel="nofollow">15.10.6. </dd></dl>
</div>
<p>This chapter will be of interest only to those building and developing HBase (i.e., as opposed to just downloading the latest distribution).</p>
<div class="section" title="15.1. HBase Repositories" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px; clear:both">
<a target="_blank" name="repos"></a>15.1. HBase 版本库</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="15.1.1. SVN" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="svn"></a>15.1.1. SVN</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">svn co http://svn.apache.org/repos/asf/hbase/trunk hbase-core-trunk 
        </pre>
</div>
<div class="section" title="15.1.2. Git" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="git"></a>15.1.2. Git</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">git clone git://git.apache.org/hbase.git
        </pre>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="15.2. IDEs" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h2 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -62.40625px; clear:both">
<a target="_blank" name="ides"></a>15.2. IDEs</h2>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="15.2.1. Eclipse" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h3 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="eclipse"></a>15.2.1. Eclipse</h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section" title="15.2.1.1. Code Formatting" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="eclipse.code.formatting"></a>15.2.1.1. Code Formatting</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>参考 <a target="_blank" class="link" href="https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/HBASE-3678" rel="nofollow">HBASE-3678 Add Eclipse-based Apache Formatter to HBase Wiki</a> for an Eclipse formatter to help ensure your code conforms to HBase'y coding convention.
 The issue includes instructions for loading the attached formatter.</p>
<p>In addition to the automatic formatting, make sure you follow the style guidelines explained in <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#common.patch.feedback" rel="nofollow" title="15.9.5. Common Patch Feedback">Section 15.10.5,
 “Common Patch Feedback”</a></p>
<p>Also, no @author tags - that's a rule. Quality Javadoc comments are appreciated. And include the Apache license.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="15.2.1.2. Subversive Plugin" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="eclipse.svn"></a>15.2.1.2. Subversive Plugin</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Download and install the Subversive plugin.</p>
<p>Set up an SVN Repository target from <a target="_blank" class="xref" href="http://www.just4e.com/hbase.html#svn" rel="nofollow" title="15.1.1. SVN">Section 15.1.1, “SVN”</a>, then check out the code.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="15.2.1.3. Git Plugin" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="eclipse.git.plugin"></a>15.2.1.3. Git Plugin</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>If you cloned the project via git, download and install the Git plugin (EGit). Attach to your local git repo (via the Git Repositories window) and you'll be able to see file revision history, generate patches, etc.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="15.2.1.4. HBase Project Setup in Eclipse" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="eclipse.maven.setup"></a>15.2.1.4. HBase Project Setup in Eclipse</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The easiest way is to use the m2eclipse plugin for Eclipse. Eclipse Indigo or newer has m2eclipse built-in, or it can be found here:http://www.eclipse.org/m2e/. M2Eclipse provides Maven integration for Eclipse - it even lets you use the direct Maven commands
 from within Eclipse to compile and test your project.</p>
<p>To import the project, you merely need to go to File-&gt;Import...Maven-&gt;Existing Maven Projects and then point Eclipse at the HBase root directory; m2eclipse will automatically find all the hbase modules for you.</p>
<p>If you install m2eclipse and import HBase in your workspace, you will have to fix your eclipse Build Path. Remove <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">target</code> folder, add <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">target/generated-jamon</code> and <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">target/generated-sources/java</code> folders.
 You may also remove from your Build Path the exclusions on the <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">src/main/resources</code> and <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">src/test/resources</code> to avoid error message in the console
 'Failed to execute goal org.apache.maven.plugins:maven-antrun-plugin:1.6:run (default) on project hbase: 'An Ant BuildException has occured: Replace: source file .../target/classes/hbase-default.xml doesn't exist'. This will also reduce the eclipse build cycles
 and make your life easier when developing.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="15.2.1.5. Import into eclipse with the command line" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="eclipse.commandline"></a>15.2.1.5. Import into eclipse with the command line</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>For those not inclined to use m2eclipse, you can generate the Eclipse files from the command line. First, run (you should only have to do this once):</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">mvn clean install -DskipTests</pre>
<p>and then close Eclipse and execute...</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">mvn eclipse:eclipse</pre>
<p>... from your local HBase project directory in your workspace to generate some new <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">.project</code> and <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">.classpath</code>files. Then reopen Eclipse, and import
 the .project file in the HBase directory to a workspace.</p>
</div>
<div class="section" title="15.2.1.6. Maven Classpath Variable" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="eclipse.maven.class"></a>15.2.1.6. Maven Classpath Variable</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <code class="varname">M2_REPO</code> classpath variable needs to be set up for the project. This needs to be set to your local Maven repository, which is usually <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">~/.m2/repository</code></p>
If this classpath variable is not configured, you will see compile errors in Eclipse like this...
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">Description	Resource	Path	Location	Type
The project cannot be built until build path errors are resolved	hbase		Unknown	Java Problem 
Unbound classpath variable: 'M2_REPO/asm/asm/3.1/asm-3.1.jar' in project 'hbase'	hbase		Build path	Build Path Problem
Unbound classpath variable: 'M2_REPO/com/github/stephenc/high-scale-lib/high-scale-lib/1.1.1/high-scale-lib-1.1.1.jar' in project 'hbase'	hbase		Build path	Build Path Problem 
Unbound classpath variable: 'M2_REPO/com/google/guava/guava/r09/guava-r09.jar' in project 'hbase'	hbase		Build path	Build Path Problem
Unbound classpath variable: 'M2_REPO/com/google/protobuf/protobuf-java/2.3.0/protobuf-java-2.3.0.jar' in project 'hbase'	hbase		Build path	Build Path Problem Unbound classpath variable:
            </pre>
</div>
<div class="section" title="15.2.1.7. Eclipse Known Issues" style="margin:0px">
<div class="titlepage" style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<div style="margin:0px">
<h4 class="title" style="color:rgb(153,0,0); line-height:1.3; margin:0.8em 0px 0px -46.8125px">
<a target="_blank" name="eclipse.issues"></a>15.2.1.7. Eclipse Known Issues</h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Eclipse will currently complain about <code class="filename" style="color:rgb(0,122,0)">Bytes.java</code>. It is not possible to turn these errors off.</p>
<pre class="programlisting" style="margin-top:0.75em; margin-bottom:0.75em; line-height:1; padding:1ex; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); background-color:rgb(238,238,238)">            
Description	Resource	Path	Location	Type
Access restriction: The method arrayBaseOffset(Class) from the type Unsafe is not accessible due to restriction on required library /System/Library/Java/JavaVirtualMachines/1.6.0.jdk/Contents/Classes/classes.jar	Bytes.java	/hbase/src/main/java/org/apache/hadoop/hbase/util	line 1061	Java Problem
Access restriction: The method arrayIndexScale(Class) from the type Unsafe is not accessible due to restriction on required library /System/Library/Java/JavaVirtualMachines/1.6.0.jdk/Contents/Classes/classes.jar	Bytes.java	/hbase/src/main/java/org/apache/hadoop/hbase/util	line 1064	Java Problem
